<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">冪</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">跳到导航</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">跳到搜索</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="zh"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E6%B6%88%E6%AD%A7%E4%B9%89" title="Wikipedia:消歧义"><img alt="Confusion grey.svg" data-file-height="200" data-file-width="260" decoding="async" height="18" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Confusion_grey.svg/24px-Confusion_grey.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Confusion_grey.svg/36px-Confusion_grey.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Confusion_grey.svg/48px-Confusion_grey.svg.png 2x" width="24"/></a><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r74030214">body:not(.skin-minerva) .mw-parser-output .ifmobile>.mobile{display:none}body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .ifmobile>.nomobile{display:inherit;display:initial}</style><span class="ifmobile"><span class="nomobile">  </span><span class="mobile"></span></span><b>提示</b>：此条目的主题不是<b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A5%8A%E5%86%AA" title="楊冪">楊冪</a></b>。</div>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E6%B6%88%E6%AD%A7%E4%B9%89" title="Wikipedia:消歧义"><img alt="Disambig gray.svg" data-file-height="168" data-file-width="220" decoding="async" height="19" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/25px-Disambig_gray.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/38px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Disambig_gray.svg/50px-Disambig_gray.svg.png 2x" width="25"/></a><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r74030214" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="ifmobile"><span class="nomobile">  </span><span class="mobile"></span></span>此条目的主題是代数概念。關於几何定理，請見「<b><a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E5%B9%82%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="圆幂定理">圆幂定理</a></b>」。</div>

<div class="noteTA" id="noteTA-307af9e9"><div class="noteTA-group"><div data-noteta-group="Math" data-noteta-group-source="module"></div></div></div>
<p><b>幂運算</b>（英語：<span lang="en">exponentiation</span>），又稱<b>指數運算</b>，是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8" title="數學">數學</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%81%8B%E7%AE%97" title="運算">運算</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E8%A1%A8%E9%81%94%E5%BC%8F" title="表達式">表達式</a>為 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle b^{n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8f8f52cd26bb201e02c8d1b3619a3a682f44dbc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.216ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>，讀作“<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 的 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 次方”或「<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 的 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 次幂」。其中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 稱為<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%95%E6%95%B0" title="底数">底數</a>，而 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 稱為<a href="/wiki/%E6%8C%87%E6%95%B0" title="指数">指數</a>，通常指數寫成<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8A%E6%A8%99" title="上標">上標</a>，放在底數的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%B3%E8%BE%B9" title="右边">右邊</a>。當不能用上標時，例如在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B7%A8%E7%A8%8B%E8%AA%9E%E8%A8%80" title="編程語言">編程語言</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AD%90%E9%83%B5%E4%BB%B6" title="電子郵件">電子郵件</a>中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle b^{n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8f8f52cd26bb201e02c8d1b3619a3a682f44dbc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.216ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> 通常寫成 <b>b^n</b> 或 <b>b**n</b>；也可視為<a href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E8%BF%90%E7%AE%97" title="超运算">超運算</a>，記為 <b>b[3]n</b>；亦可以用<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E5%BE%B7%E7%B4%8D%E7%AE%AD%E8%99%9F%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E6%B3%95" title="高德納箭號表示法">高德納箭號表示法</a>，寫成 <b>b↑n</b>。
</p><p>若<i>n</i>為<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E6%95%B4%E6%95%B8" title="正整數">正整數</a>，可以把 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle b^{n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8f8f52cd26bb201e02c8d1b3619a3a682f44dbc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.216ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span> 看作乘方的结果，等同於 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 自乘 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 次。
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{n}=\underbrace {b\times \cdots \times b} _{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{n}=\underbrace {b\times \cdots \times b} _{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b^{n}=\underbrace {b\times \cdots \times b}_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b68c9079cbad49c59181e2fc446d36f550b542e9" style="vertical-align: -3.671ex; margin-right: -0.028ex; width:15.741ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>當指數為 1 時，通常不寫出來，因為運算出的值和底數的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%80%BC" title="数值">數值</a>一樣；指數為 2 時，可以讀作“<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E6%95%B0" title="平方数">平方</a>”；指數為 3 時，可以讀作“<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AB%8B%E6%96%B9%E6%95%B0" title="立方数">立方</a>”。
</p><p>起始值 1（乘法的<a href="/wiki/%E5%96%AE%E4%BD%8D%E5%85%83" title="單位元">單位元</a>）乘上底數（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>）自乘指數（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>）這麼多次。這樣<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89" title="定义">定義</a>了後，很易想到如何一般化指數 0 和負數的情況：除 0 外所有數的零次方都是 1 ；指數是負數時就等於重複<a href="/wiki/%E9%99%A4%E6%B3%95" title="除法">除以</a>底數（或底數的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%80%92%E6%95%B8" title="倒數">倒數</a>自乘指數這麼多次），即：
</p>

<p>以<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%95%B8" title="分數">分數</a>為指數的冪定義為 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{\frac {m}{n}}={\sqrt[{n}]{b^{m}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mfrac>

</semantics>

</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> 次<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="方根">方根</a>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/0%E7%9A%840%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9" title="0的0次方">0的0次方</a>目前沒有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%AE%B6" title="數學家">數學家</a>給予正式的定義。在部分<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E9%A0%98%E5%9F%9F" title="數學領域">數學領域</a>中，如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B5%84%E5%90%88%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8" title="組合數學">組合數學</a>，常用的慣例是定義為 1 ，也有人主張定義為 1 。
</p><p>因為在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%81%E8%BF%9B%E5%88%B6" title="十进制">十进制</a>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%81%E7%9A%84%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9" title="十的次方">十的次方</a>很易計算，只需在後面加零即可，所以<a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E8%AE%B0%E6%95%B0%E6%B3%95" title="科学记数法">科学记数法</a>借此<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B0%A1%E5%8C%96" title="簡化">簡化</a><a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%B0%E5%BD%95" title="记录">記錄</a>的數字；<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%B9%82" title="二的幂">二的幂</a>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A8%88%E7%AE%97%E6%A9%9F%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%B8" title="計算機科學">計算機科學</a>相當重要。
</p><p>當<i>n</i>是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A4%87%E6%95%B8_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="複數 (數學)">複數</a>及<i>b</i>是正實數時,
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{n}=\exp(n\ln(b))}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>

<mi>exp</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>n</mi>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{n}=\exp(n\ln(b))}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle b^{n}=\exp(n\ln(b))}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/75cf1ee7d21184df706654ddf1de6a86ada1efb5" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.204ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>exp 是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%8C%87%E6%95%B8%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="指數函數">指數函數</a>而 ln 是<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E5%B0%8D%E6%95%B8" title="自然對數">自然對數</a>。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E9.87.8D.E8.A6.81.E7.9A.84.E6.81.86.E7.AD.89.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="重要的恆等式">重要的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%81%86%E7%AD%89%E5%BC%8F" title="恆等式">恆等式</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：重要的恆等式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E8.BF.90.E7.AE.97.E6.B3.95.E5.88.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="运算法则">运算法则</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：运算法则">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>同底数幂相乘，底数不变，指数相加：</li></ul>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{m}\times a^{n}=a^{m+n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<ul><li>同底数幂相除，底数不变，指数相减：</li></ul>

<h2><span id=".E8.BF.90.E7.AE.97.E5.BE.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="运算律">运算律</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：运算律">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>加法和乘法存在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E6%8D%A2%E5%BE%8B" title="交换律">交换律</a>，比如：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2+3=5=3+2}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>5</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2+3=5=3+2}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 2+3=5=3+2}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a9cd9dd28cbc83eae65420bcdac5f0e9e193ddaa" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:17.69ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2\times 3=6=3\times 2}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>6</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mn>2</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2\times 3=6=3\times 2}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 2\times 3=6=3\times 2}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f4b41199dae87f98b9787fb1d43f002ebc9981f6" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:17.69ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，但是幂的运算不存在交换律，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2^{3}=8}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>2</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>8</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2^{3}=8}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="2^3 = 8 " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bb2dded8eba905e4a019b70abad935422b198db4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.478ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>，但是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3^{2}=9}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>3</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>9</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 3^{2}=9}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="3^2 = 9 " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6ce3bb0717e9aa3fd7c54d6676a7a7fe15e78e66" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.478ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>同样，加法和乘法存在<a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%BE%8B" title="结合律">结合律</a>，比如：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (2+3)+4=9=2+(3+4)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>+</mo>
<mn>4</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>9</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mn>4</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (2+3)+4=9=2+(3+4)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (2+3)+4=9=2+(3+4)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bc7ea3321860682433db583f2b13c188e58d7478" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:29.314ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (2\times 3)\times 4=24=2\times (3\times 4)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>

<h2><span id=".E6.95.B4.E6.95.B0.E6.8C.87.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="整数指数幂">整数指数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：整数指数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>整数指数幂的运算只需要<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%9D%E7%AD%89%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0" title="初等代数">初等代数</a>的知识。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.AD.A3.E6.95.B4.E6.95.B0.E6.8C.87.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="正整数指数幂">正整数指数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：正整数指数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>表达式<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{2}=a\cdot a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{2}=a\cdot a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^2 = a\cdot a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a5e07183677e63dfd13c0aab13607bcc848df906" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:9.521ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>被称作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9" title="平方">平方</a>，因为边长为<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>的正方形面积是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^2" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f564e5dc0b6e68af32ca8614e972f5b36e944a24" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.284ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>表达式<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{3}=a\cdot a\cdot a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{3}=a\cdot a\cdot a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^3 = a\cdot a\cdot a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b9a55547d76a225c949dc5ab450ca47750860fb7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:12.43ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>被称作<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AB%8B%E6%96%B9%E6%95%B0" title="立方数">立方</a>，因为邊长为<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>的正方体体积是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{3}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{3}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^3" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/abd83c98f7301a720f69dd6d4043461e4cc83daa" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.284ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>所以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>3</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 3^{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="3^2" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/84cba38173d6b69364f2016245721c333282e0d7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.217ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>读作「3的平方」，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2^{3}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>2</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2^{3}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="2^3" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/52e9f8299773e9205d2055998f3c8eb9441877fc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.217ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>读作「2的立方」。
</p><p>指数表示的是底数反复相乘多少次。比如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3^{5}=3\times 3\times 3\times 3\times 3=243}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>3</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>5</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>243</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 3^{5}=3\times 3\times 3\times 3\times 3=243}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="3^5 = 3\times 3\times 3\times 3\times 3 = 243" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4a81cadf3224a29e7b04f428675e7167f091e7a7" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:29.075ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>，指数是5，底数是3，表示3反复相乘5次。
</p><p>或者，整数指数幂可以<a href="/wiki/%E9%80%92%E5%BD%92" title="递归">递归</a>地定义成：
</p>

<h3><span id=".E6.8C.87.E6.95.B0.E6.98.AF1.E6.88.96.E8.80.850"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="指数是1或者0">指数是1或者0</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：指数是1或者0">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>注意<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3^{1}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</p><p>注意<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3^{5}=3\times 3^{4}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>

<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<msup>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</p><p>继续，得到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3^{1}=3\times 3^{0}=3}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>3</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<msup>
<mn>3</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 3^{1}=3\times 3^{0}=3}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="3^1 = 3\times 3^0 = 3" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7ad178a7c0599ba415b93d743792ed1d24b30a52" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:15.796ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>，所以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3^{0}=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>3</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 3^{0}=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="3^0 = 1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1dad67a3175417e73e1ec7b2970163ad97157b1e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.478ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>
</p><p>另一个得到此结论的方法是：通过运算法则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{n}}{x^{m}}}=x^{n-m}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>m</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>m</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{n}}{x^{m}}}=x^{n-m}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt=" \frac{x^n}{x^m} = x^{n - m}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/00a6304ef64ac96ef0d76cb8fabc010e9759756d" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:12.209ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>
</p><p>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m=n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>m</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle m=n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="m=n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/69c9d8e54796e7de7d4738510cc10bc3fc55d48e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.534ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>时，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1={\frac {x^{n}}{x^{n}}}=x^{n-n}=x^{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 1={\frac {x^{n}}{x^{n}}}=x^{n-n}=x^{0}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt=" 1 = \frac{x^n}{x^n} = x^{n - n} = x^0 " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e2a3813abd81904297c593d1ea9005391e2e206" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:21.039ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>
</p>
<ul><li>任何数的<b>1</b>次方是它本身。</li></ul>
<h3><span id=".E9.9B.B6.E7.9A.84.E9.9B.B6.E6.AC.A1.E6.96.B9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="零的零次方">零的零次方</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：零的零次方">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%B6%E7%9A%84%E9%9B%B6%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9" title="零的零次方">零的零次方</a></div>
<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0^{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>0</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0^{0}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt=" 0^0 " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/106f0c4e1cbccbfcbb61001a8c17b8427c65366d" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.217ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span> 其实还并未被数学家完整的定义，但部分看法是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0^{0}=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>0</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0^{0}=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt=" 0^0 = 1 " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/478100bc5766c6af537439ef9309f9ddf2f9a6ff" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.478ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span> ，在程式语言中（python） <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0**0=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>0</mn>
<mo>∗<!-- ∗ --></mo>
<mo>∗<!-- ∗ --></mo>
<mn>0</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0**0=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 0**0=1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/61b4567c41f1b63ced736e3e25b8ec9eb296b7b8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:9.943ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>
</p><p>在这里给出这一种极限的看法
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{x\to 0^{+}}x^{x}=0^{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.B4.9F.E6.95.B0.E6.8C.87.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="负数指数">负数指数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：负数指数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>我们定义任何不为<b> 0 </b>的数<b> a </b>的<b> -1 </b>次方等于它的倒数。
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{-1}={\frac {1}{a}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mi>a</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{-1}={\frac {1}{a}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle a^{-1}={\frac {1}{a}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/782fa7c46e15fbb82c9002f8c9f72a3fceb8007f" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:8.727ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>对于非零<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{-n}={\frac {1}{a^{n}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>而<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>证法一：
</p><p>根据定义<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{m}\cdot a^{n}=a^{m+n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</msup>

<p>得<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{-n}\,a^{n}=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>

</p><p>证法二：
</p><p>通过运算法则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {a^{m}}{a^{n}}}=a^{m-n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</msup>
</mfrac>

<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {a^{m}}{a^{n}}}=a^{m-n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {a^{m}}{a^{n}}}=a^{m-n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/884018dbd9271fc772f0196f0db1c63cd2f8a211" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:12.009ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>
</p><p>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>负数指数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{-n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。比如：
</p>

</mfrac>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 3^{-4}={\frac {\frac {\frac {\frac {1}{3}}{3}}{3}}{3}}={\frac {1}{81}}={\frac {1}{3^{4}}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="3^{{-4}}={\frac  {{\frac  {{\frac  {{\frac  {1}{3}}}{3}}}{3}}}{3}}={\frac  {1}{81}}={\frac  {1}{3^{{4}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/566c3f4e56f0b307c3dfdb8057d7c4a76a5c825f" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:23.016ex; height:10.343ex;"/></span>.</dd></dl>
<h3><span id=".E7.89.B9.E6.AE.8A.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="特殊数的幂">特殊数的幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：特殊数的幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="10.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="10的幂">10的幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：10的幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E8%AE%A1%E6%95%B0%E6%B3%95" title="科学计数法">科学计数法</a></div>
<p>在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%81%E8%BF%9B%E5%88%B6" title="十进制">十进制</a>的计数系统中，10的幂写成1后面跟着很多个0。例如：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 10^{3}=1000,\ 10^{-3}=0.001}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>10</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1000</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
<msup>
<mn>10</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0.001</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 10^{3}=1000,\ 10^{-3}=0.001}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="10^3 = 1000,\ 10^{-3} = 0.001" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/82df408d950122601211f711d1bbd1e09c720921" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:25.795ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>
</p><p>因此10的幂用来表示非常大或者非常小的数字。如：299,792,458（真空中<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%89%E9%80%9F" title="光速">光速</a>，单位是<a href="/wiki/%E7%B1%B3%E6%AF%8F%E7%A7%92" title="米每秒">米每秒</a>），可以写成 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2.99792458\times 10^{8}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>2.99792458</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<msup>
<mn>10</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>8</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2.99792458\times 10^{8}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="2.99792458\times 10^8" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1d2f523f8614d72d08d6be9025ef08062ac4527b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:17.328ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E5%80%BC" title="近似值">近似值</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2.998\times 10^{8}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>2.998</mn>
<mo>×<!-- × --></mo>
<msup>
<mn>10</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>8</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>

</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2.998\times 10^{8}}</annotation>
</semantics>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 3\times 10^{8}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 3\times 10^{8}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2eea2f21ef938c2997e908705650f066afb9b22d" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.382ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E5%88%B6%E8%AF%8D%E5%A4%B4" title="国际单位制词头">国际单位制词头</a>也使用10的幂来描述特别大或者特别小的数字，比如：词头“千”就是 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 10^{3}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h4><span id="2.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2的幂">2的幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：2的幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/2%E7%9A%84%E5%B9%82" title="2的幂">2的幂</a></div>
<h4><span id="1.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1的幂">1的幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：1的幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>1的任何次幂都为1
</p>
<h4><span id="0.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="0的幂">0的幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：0的幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>0的正数幂都等于0。
</p><p>0的负数幂没有定义。
</p><p>任何非0之数的0次方都是1；而<a href="/wiki/0%E7%9A%840%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9" title="0的0次方">0的0次方</a>是懸而未決的，某些領域下常用的慣例是約定為1。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup>但某些教科書表示0的0次方為無意義。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup>也有人主張定義為1。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E8.B4.9F1.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="负1的幂">负1的幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：负1的幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>-1的奇数幂等于-1
</p><p>-1的偶数幂等于1
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.8C.87.E6.95.B0.E9.9D.9E.E5.B8.B8.E5.A4.A7.E6.97.B6.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="指数非常大时的幂">指数非常大时的幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：指数非常大时的幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>一个大于1的数的幂趋于<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E5%A4%A7" title="无穷大">无穷大</a>，一个小于-1的数的幂趋于负无穷大
</p>
<dl><dd>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a&gt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>一个绝对值小于1的数的幂趋于0
</p>
<dl><dd>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle |a|&lt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>1的幂永远都是1
</p>
<dl><dd>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a = 1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6104442ed30596ef4d7795d3186273f68d796ea4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.491ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n\to \infty }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n\to \infty }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt=" n \to \infty" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a0d55d9b32f6fa8fab6a84ea444a6b5a24bb45e1" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.333ex; height:1.843ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{n}\to 1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>

<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{n}\to 1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt=" a^n \to 1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2e6750087b2ef3e4be0866ea75eef1c96a4e672c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.225ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>如果数<i>a</i>趋于1而它的幂趋于无穷，那么极限并不一定是上面几个。一个很重要的例子是：
</p>
<dl><dd>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n\to \infty ,\left(1+{\frac {1}{n}}\right)^{n}\to e}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<msup>
<mrow>
<mo>(</mo>
<mrow>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mi>n</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mrow>
<mo>)</mo>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mi>e</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n\to \infty ,\left(1+{\frac {1}{n}}\right)^{n}\to e}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n\to \infty ,\left(1+{\frac  {1}{n}}\right)^{n}\to e" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0aa42189272edc95e9798cdb7cc82042623719a8" style="vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:23.937ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>参见<a href="#e的幂">e的幂</a>
</p><p>其他指数的极限参见<a href="#幂的极限">幂的极限</a>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.AD.A3.E5.AE.9E.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.AE.9E.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="正实数的实数幂">正实数的实数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="编辑章节：正实数的实数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>一个正实数的<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0" title="实数">实数</a>幂可以通过两种方法实现。
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="有理数">有理数</a>幂可以通过N次<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="方根">方根</a>定义，任何非0实数次幂都可以这样定义</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0" title="自然对数">自然对数</a>可以被用来通过指数函数定义实数幂</li></ul>
<h3><span id="N.E6.AC.A1.E6.96.B9.E6.A0.B9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="N次方根">N次方根</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="编辑章节：N次方根">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p>一个<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0" title="数">数</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>

<mi>n</mi>

</mrow>

</semantics>

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x^n=a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d4f72f2b21e69fe32e9d348b1768bb5bd017fa1b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.876ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>如果<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x^{n}=a}</annotation>
</semantics>

这个根被称为<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>次方根也可以写成<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{\frac {1}{n}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

例如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 4^{\frac {1}{2}}=2,\ 8^{\frac {1}{3}}=2}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 4^{\frac {1}{2}}=2,\ 8^{\frac {1}{3}}=2}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="4^{\frac{1}{2}} = 2,\ 8^{\frac{1}{3}} = 2" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/97cab49d6dab261db40736957105d0d536f77328" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:15.933ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>
</p><p>当指数是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mn>2</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{2}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\frac {1}{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a11cfb2fdb143693b1daf78fcb5c11a023cb1c55" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:1.999ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>时根号上的2可以省略，如：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {4}}=4^{\frac {1}{2}}={\sqrt[{2}]{4}}=2}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mn>4</mn>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mn>4</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mn>2</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mroot>
<mn>4</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</mroot>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {4}}=4^{\frac {1}{2}}={\sqrt[{2}]{4}}=2}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {4}}=4^{\frac {1}{2}}={\sqrt[{2}]{4}}=2}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/90efca0389d4fc157651b7d95aacf2c8320b9ddd" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:19.553ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.9C.89.E7.90.86.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="有理数幂">有理数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="编辑章节：有理数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>有理数指数幂定义为
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{\frac {m}{n}}=(a^{m})^{\frac {1}{n}}={\sqrt[{n}]{a^{m}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>n</mi>

<h3><span id="e.E7.9A.84.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="e的幂">e的幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="编辑章节：e的幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%8C%87%E6%95%B0%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="指数函数">指数函数</a></div>
<p>这个重要的数学常数<a href="/wiki/E_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%B8%B8%E6%95%B0)" title="E (数学常数)"><i>e</i></a>，有时叫做<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E6%95%B0" title="欧拉数">欧拉数</a>，近似2.718，是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0" title="自然对数">自然对数</a>的底。它提供了定义非整数指数幂的一个方法。
它是从以下极限定义的：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e=\lim _{n\to \infty }\left(1+{\frac {1}{n}}\right)^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e^{x}=\lim _{n\to \infty }\left(1+{\frac {x}{n}}\right)^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
