<h3><span id=".E5.AE.9E.E6.95.B0.E6.8C.87.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="实数指数幂">实数指数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="编辑章节：实数指数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:317px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Expo02.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="315" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Expo02.svg/315px-Expo02.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Expo02.svg/473px-Expo02.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Expo02.svg/630px-Expo02.svg.png 2x" width="315"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Expo02.svg" title="放大"></a></div><span class="nowrap">y = b<sup>x</sup></span>對各種底數b的圖像，分別為綠色的10、紅色的e、藍色的2和青色的1/2。</div></div></div>
<p>因为所有<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0" title="实数">实数</a>可以近似地表示为有理数，任意实数指数<i>x</i>可以定义成<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Denlinger_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-Denlinger-3">[3]</a></sup>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{x}=\lim _{r\to x}b^{r},}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<munder>
<mo form="prefix" movablelimits="true">lim</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>r</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</munder>
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>r</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>,</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{x}=\lim _{r\to x}b^{r},}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt=" b^x = \lim_{r \to x} b^r," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3776851baeb79dfe2d74aa00705642145575b1c8" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:11.599ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>例如：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x\approx 1.732}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>≈<!-- ≈ --></mo>
<mn>1.732</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x\approx 1.732}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x \approx 1.732 " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8a37965b060468689973e1b6728529b692913876" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:9.725ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>于是
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 5^{x}\approx 5^{1.732}=5^{\frac {433}{250}}={\sqrt[{250}]{5^{433}}}\approx 16.241}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mn>5</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>≈<!-- ≈ --></mo>
<msup>
<mn>5</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1.732</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mn>5</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>433</mn>
<mn>250</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mroot>
<msup>
<mn>5</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>433</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>250</mn>
</mrow>
</mroot>
</mrow>
<mo>≈<!-- ≈ --></mo>
<mn>16.241</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 5^{x}\approx 5^{1.732}=5^{\frac {433}{250}}={\sqrt[{250}]{5^{433}}}\approx 16.241}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="5^{x}\approx 5^{{1.732}}=5^{{{\frac  {433}{250}}}}={\sqrt[ {250}]{5^{{433}}}}\approx 16.241" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bdf754bc1958eba28bd5b9f85aed46c01e62a4d8" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:37.183ex; height:4.009ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>实数指数幂通常使用对数来定义，而不是近似有理数。
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0" title="自然对数">自然对数</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \ln {x}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \ln {x}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\ln{x} " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68c47eeb7700e9adf786e4f4db84a6911c9a3b8a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.656ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是指数函数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e^{x}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e^{x}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e^{x}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/841c0d168e64191c45a45e54c7e447defd17ec6a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.256ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="反函數">反函数</a>。
它的定义是：对于任意<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b&gt;0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
<mo>&gt;</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b&gt;0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b&gt;0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/94436473a90bd55191a79c59474cb5456dcbec00" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.258ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，满足
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b=e^{\ln b}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>b</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b=e^{\ln b}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b = e^{\ln b}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a611fee78d56f820024010fb8dadb1e0742bc0b2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.876ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>根据对数和指数运算的规则：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{x}=(e^{\ln b})^{x}=e^{x\cdot \ln b}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>b</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>b</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{x}=(e^{\ln b})^{x}=e^{x\cdot \ln b}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b^x = (e^{\ln b})^x = e^{x \cdot\ln b}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fbdcf43bdd20d57ba53b5d752bd0ac7146d3a947" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:20.305ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>这就是实数指数幂的定义：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{x}=e^{x\cdot \ln b}\,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>b</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{x}=e^{x\cdot \ln b}\,}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b^x = e^{x\cdot\ln b}\," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5368832e98ba1bf141533c0860dd9be119c1426c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:10.833ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>实数指数幂<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b^{x}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{x}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b^x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2bb7406a338fb530330582bc63420d091897c709" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.17ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>的这个定义和上面使用有理数指数和连续性的定义相吻合。对于复数，这种定义更加常用。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E8.B4.9F.E5.AE.9E.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.AE.9E.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="负实数的实数幂">负实数的实数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="编辑章节：负实数的实数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>如果<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是负数且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%81%B6%E6%95%B0" title="偶数">偶数</a>，那么<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x=a^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x=a^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle x=a^{n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/407e45335787b25bf78954908ec685cfb6b23622" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.876ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>是正數。如果<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>是负数且<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A5%87%E6%95%B0" title="奇数">奇数</a>，那么<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x=a^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x=a^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle x=a^{n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/407e45335787b25bf78954908ec685cfb6b23622" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.876ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>是负数。
</p><p>使用对数和有理数指数都不能将<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{k}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>k</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{k}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^k" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/79e30fb4fe7c63445f6f0f433e87ae65d87ff55f" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.319ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>（其中<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>是负实数，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle k}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>k</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle k}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="k" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3c9a2c7b599b37105512c5d570edc034056dd40" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>实数）定义成实数。在一些特殊情况下，给出一个定义是可行的：负指数的整数指数幂是实数，有理数指数幂对于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{\frac {m}{n}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>m</mi>
<mi>n</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{\frac {m}{n}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^\frac{m}{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4a712a805a8e616dd50760a69c159450bf16e59c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.47ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是奇数）可以使用<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>

</p><p>使用对数的方法不能定义<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a\leq 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>使用有理数指数幂来逼近的方法也不能用于负数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -1^{q}=-1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="-1^q=-1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3ab1d752b62e82d1696672d67e58959ea00da4c9" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:10.028ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="集合 (数学)">集合</a>也是。所以函数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle -1^{q}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<msup>
<mn>1</mn>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>q</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -1^{q}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="-1^q" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f385f8dcb6a703f6fa621e4649fb42d260991b5d" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:3.959ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>在有理数域不是连续的。
</p><p>因此，如果要求负实数的任意实数幂，必须将底数和指数看成<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A4%87%E6%95%B8_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="複數 (數學)">複數</a>，按复数的正实数幂或复数的复数幂方法计算。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.AD.A3.E5.AE.9E.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="正实数的复数幂">正实数的复数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="编辑章节：正实数的复数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="e.E7.9A.84.E8.99.9A.E6.95.B0.E6.AC.A1.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="e的虚数次幂">e的虚数次幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="编辑章节：e的虚数次幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%8C%87%E6%95%B0%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="指数函数">指数函数</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ExpIPi.gif"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="323" data-file-width="360" decoding="async" height="269" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/ExpIPi.gif/300px-ExpIPi.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/0e/ExpIPi.gif 1.5x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ExpIPi.gif" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E6%8C%87%E6%95%B0%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="指数函数">指数函数</a><i>e</i><sup><i>z</i></sup>可以通过<span class="nowrap">(1 + <i>z</i>/<i>N</i>)<sup><i>N</i></sup></span>当<i>N</i>趋于无穷大时的<a href="/wiki/%E6%A5%B5%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B8%E5%88%97)" title="極限 (數列)">极限</a>来定义，那么<i>e</i><sup><i>iπ</i></sup>就是<span class="nowrap">(1 + <i>iπ</i>/<i>N</i>)<sup><i>N</i></sup></span>的极限。在这个动画中<i>n</i>从1取到100。<span class="nowrap">(1 + <i>iπ</i>/<i>N</i>)<sup><i>N</i></sup></span>的值通过<i>N</i>重复增加在复数平面上展示，最终结果就是<span class="nowrap">(1 + <i>iπ</i>/<i>N</i>)<sup><i>N</i></sup></span>的准确值。可以看出，随着<i>N</i>的增大，<span class="nowrap">(1 + <i>iπ</i>/<i>N</i>)<sup><i>N</i></sup></span>逐渐逼近极限-1。这就是<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="欧拉公式">欧拉公式</a>。</div></div></div>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A4%87%E6%95%B8_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)" title="複數 (數學)">複數</a>运算的几何意义和<a href="#e的幂"><i>e</i>的幂</a>可以帮助我们理解<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e^{ix}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>等式<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e^{z}=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e^{z}=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e^z = 1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6f332fe026fcc9c4eb1a1e58e292a2d0ed961769" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.346ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>的解是一个整数乘以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2i\pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<h3><span id=".E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="三角函数">三角函数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="编辑章节：三角函数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="欧拉公式">欧拉公式</a></div>
<p>根据<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="欧拉公式">欧拉公式</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="三角函数">三角函数</a>余弦和正弦是： 
</p>

</p>

<p>使用了复数指数幂之后，很多三角学问题都能够使用代数方法解决。

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e^{x+iy}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e^{x+iy}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e99519a420cad88b5468c901d6bc56acc53d4fe4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.919ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>的方向
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.AD.A3.E5.AE.9E.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="正实数的复数幂_2">正实数的复数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="编辑章节：正实数的复数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>如果<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是一个正实数，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf368e72c009decd9b6686ee84a375632e11de98" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.088ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是任何复数，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{z}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{z}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^z" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6fda5d4b98ad1b1ded1a08a12990ef6f0e40316b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.231ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>定义成<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e^{z\cdot \ln(a)}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e^{z\cdot \ln(a)}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e^{z\cdot \ln(a)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4a067845a08975dc582d3633b663f7e7c7ae023b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.063ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x=\ln(a)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x=\ln(a)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle x=\ln(a)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5c9e24295651cb5baac6ef2936fe061c0f3a01d0" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:9.407ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>是方程<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e^{x}=a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e^{x}=a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e^x = a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0e12de39d381002caa0a421d26d003652bc437b2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.584ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>的唯一解。所以处理实数的方法同样可以用来处理复数。
</p><p>例如：
</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="复数的复数幂">复数的复数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="编辑章节：复数的复数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E8.A4.87.E6.95.B8.E7.9A.84.E8.99.9A.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="複數的虚数幂">複數的虚数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="编辑章节：複數的虚数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>让我们从一个简单的例子开始：计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left(1+i\right)^{i}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {2}}^{i}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {2}}^{i}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bef406c504eba87ea65618df79ba20310656a6df" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.898ex; height:3.343ex;"/></span>的得法参见上文<a href="/wiki/%E5%86%AA#正实数的复数幂_2" title="冪">正实数的复数幂</a>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E5.B9.82_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="复数的复数幂_2">复数的复数幂</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：复数的复数幂">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>类似地，在计算复数的复数幂时，我们可以将指数的实部与虚部分开以进行幂计算。例如计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left(1+i\right)^{2+i}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mrow>
<mo>(</mo>
<mrow>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>i</mi>
</mrow>
<mo>)</mo>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>i</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \left(1+i\right)^{2+i}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \left(1+i\right)^{2+i}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f14336ab97fd1e8974e2da43874290691717793d" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:9.515ex; height:3.343ex;"/></span>：
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{aligned}\left(1+i\right)^{2+i}&amp;=\left(1+i\right)^{2}\left(1+i\right)^{i}\\&amp;=2ie^{-{\tfrac {\pi }{4}}}\left(\cos {\frac {\ln 2}{2}}+i\sin {\frac {\ln 2}{2}}\right)\\&amp;=-2e^{-{\tfrac {\pi }{4}}}\sin {\frac {\ln 2}{2}}+2ie^{-{\tfrac {\pi }{4}}}\cos {\frac {\ln 2}{2}}\\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.B8.80.E8.88.AC.E6.83.85.E5.86.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="一般情况"><b>一般情况</b></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="编辑章节：一般情况">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>复数的复数幂必须首先化为底数为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cd253103f0876afc68ebead27a5aa9867d927467" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.083ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的形式：
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle w^{z}=e^{z\ln w}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>w</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>w</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle w^{z}=e^{z\ln w}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle w^{z}=e^{z\ln w}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/526d0202ac984d9a4808995b88cd047b2e6bc31c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:11.172ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>
</p><p>又，由复数的极坐标表示法：
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle w=re^{i\theta }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>w</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>r</mi>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>i</mi>
<mi>θ<!-- θ --></mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle w=re^{i\theta }}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="w=re^{{i\theta }}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/066804c476b780efde6168a0d37c008c701b3c3e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:8.465ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>
</p><p>故
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle w^{z}=e^{z\ln(w)}=e^{z(\ln(r)+i\theta )}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>w</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>w</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>z</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>ln</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>r</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>i</mi>
<mi>θ<!-- θ --></mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle w^{z}=e^{z\ln(w)}=e^{z(\ln(r)+i\theta )}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle w^{z}=e^{z\ln(w)}=e^{z(\ln(r)+i\theta )}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/31b3aad9b9b78fb6cc5245356f6a4329cfe717db" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:24.536ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>然后，使用<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="欧拉公式">欧拉公式</a>处理即可。
</p><p>由于复数的极坐标表示法中，<a href="/wiki/%E8%BE%90%E8%A7%92" title="辐角">辐角</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \theta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>θ<!-- θ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \theta }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\theta " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6e5ab2664b422d53eb0c7df3b87e1360d75ad9af" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.09ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的取值是具有周期性的，因此复数的复数幂在大多数情况下是<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E5%80%BC%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="多值函数">多值函数</a>。不过实际应用中，为了简便起见，辐角都只取主值，从而使幂值唯一。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.9C.A8.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B8.E4.B8.AD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="在函數中">在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="函數">函數</a>中</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="编辑章节：在函數中">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>當函數名後有上標的數（即函數的指數），一般指要重複它的運算。例如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f^{3}(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>f</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f^{3}(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f^3 (x )" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/218b0ffd82ef0f3907e785313ec63131d5fb2bf1" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.514ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>即<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(f(f(x)))}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(f(f(x)))}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle f(f(f(x)))}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf2e7b26f65defcb29b60914b28c3199c7b77d24" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:10.593ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。特別地，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f^{-1}(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>f</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f^{-1}(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f^{-1} (x )" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/46a543a3462cbb9effd5d0c514529426172c7d7b" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.792ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>指<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f (x )" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="反函數">反函數</a>。
</p><p>但<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="三角函数">三角函数</a>的情況有所不同，一個正指數應用於函數的名字時，指答案要進行乘方運算，而指數為-1時则表示其反函數。例如：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (\sin x)^{-1}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>sin</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (\sin x)^{-1}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="(\sin x)^{-1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/562f6086f3d84b8f7bee446d4f3b1d22633a418a" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.714ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>表示<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \csc x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>csc</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \csc x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\csc x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f0e0fc784f0e9c8c3346f7891568f4ab216c1155" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.698ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。因此在三角函數時，使用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sin ^{-1}x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>sin</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sin ^{-1}x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sin^{-1} x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b43621a8bcd117b4e136e8c0b5d8a73f0bf3609a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.905ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>來表示<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sin x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>sin</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sin x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sin x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/09b4b55580d6a821a07ad9fe35be88976917b10b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.572ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的反函數<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \arcsin x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>arcsin</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \arcsin x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\arcsin x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8941574c0f224adeedae0f72bd48098116cc2068" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.679ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.9C.A8.E6.8A.BD.E8.B1.A1.E4.BB.A3.E6.95.B8.E4.B8.AD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="在抽象代數中">在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%8A%BD%E8%B1%A1%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8" title="抽象代數">抽象代數</a>中</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：在抽象代數中">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h2><span id=".E8.AE.A1.E7.AE.97.E8.87.AA.E7.84.B6.E6.95.B0.EF.BC.88.E6.AD.A3.E6.95.B4.E6.95.B0.EF.BC.89.7F.27.22.60UNIQ--postMath-000000F6-QINU.60.22.27.7F.E7.9A.84.7F.27.22.60UNIQ--postMath-000000F7-QINU.60.22.27.7F.E7.9A.84.E7.AE.97.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="计算自然数（正整数）'&quot;`UNIQ--postMath-000000F6-QINU`&quot;'的'&quot;`UNIQ--postMath-000000F7-QINU`&quot;'的算法">计算自然数（正整数）<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></i>的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2687184a7698e75db65a25bea7afd207bff3d03b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>的算法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title='编辑章节：计算自然数（正整数）&lt;span class="mwe-math-element"&gt;&lt;span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"&gt;&lt;math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle n}"&gt;
  &lt;semantics&gt;
    &lt;mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"&gt;
      &lt;mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"&gt;
        &lt;mi&gt;n&lt;/mi&gt;
      &lt;/mstyle&gt;
    &lt;/mrow&gt;
    &lt;annotation encoding="application/x-tex"&gt;{\displaystyle n}&lt;/annotation&gt;
  &lt;/semantics&gt;
&lt;/math&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="n"/&gt;&lt;/span&gt;的&lt;span class="mwe-math-element"&gt;&lt;span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"&gt;&lt;math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle a^{n}}"&gt;
  &lt;semantics&gt;
    &lt;mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"&gt;
      &lt;mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"&gt;
        &lt;msup&gt;
          &lt;mi&gt;a&lt;/mi&gt;
          &lt;mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"&gt;
            &lt;mi&gt;n&lt;/mi&gt;
          &lt;/mrow&gt;
        &lt;/msup&gt;
      &lt;/mstyle&gt;
    &lt;/mrow&gt;
    &lt;annotation encoding="application/x-tex"&gt;{\displaystyle a^{n}}&lt;/annotation&gt;
  &lt;/semantics&gt;
&lt;/math&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2687184a7698e75db65a25bea7afd207bff3d03b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="a^n"/&gt;&lt;/span&gt;的算法'>编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>最快的方式计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2687184a7698e75db65a25bea7afd207bff3d03b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>，当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是正整数的时候。它利用了测试一个数是奇数在计算机上是非常容易的，和通过简单的移所有位向右来<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%99%A4%E4%BB%A52" title="除以2">除以2</a>的事实。
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%81%BD%E4%BB%A3%E7%A2%BC" title="偽代碼">偽代碼</a>：
</p>
<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-text mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span>   1. 1 → y, n → k, a → f
   2.若k不為0,執行3至6
     3.若k為奇數, y * f → y
     4. k [[位操作#移位|右移]]1位（即k / 2 → k ,小數點無條件捨去）
     5. f * f → f
     6.回到2
   7.傳回y
</pre></div>
<p>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/C%E8%AA%9E%E8%A8%80" title="C語言">C</a>/<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/C%2B%2B%E8%AF%AD%E8%A8%80" title="C++语言">C++语言</a>中，你可以写如下算法：
</p>
<div class="mw-highlight mw-highlight-lang-c mw-content-ltr mw-highlight-lines" dir="ltr"><pre><span></span><span class="linenos" data-line="1"></span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nf">power</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kt">unsigned</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kt">int</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">n</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="2"></span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="3"></span><span class="w">    </span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">y</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="4"></span><span class="w">    </span><span class="kt">double</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">f</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="5"></span><span class="w">    </span><span class="k">while</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">n</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="6"></span><span class="w">       </span><span class="k">if</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">n</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">%</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">==</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">y</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">*=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="7"></span><span class="w">       </span><span class="n">n</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">&gt;&gt;=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="8"></span><span class="w">       </span><span class="n">f</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">*=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">f</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="9"></span><span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="10"></span><span class="w">    </span><span class="k">return</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"></span>
<span class="linenos" data-line="11"></span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"></span>
</pre></div>
<p>此算法的<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%A4%8D%E6%9D%82%E5%BA%A6" title="时间复杂度">時間複雜度</a>為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {O} (\log n)\!}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">O</mi>
</mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>log</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>n</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mspace width="negativethinmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {O} (\log n)\!}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathrm {O} (\log n)\!" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6c35c6c21c30a5643d3100b7993f907b58cf79cf" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; margin-right: -0.166ex; width:8.15ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，比普通算法快（a自乘100次，<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%A4%8D%E6%9D%82%E5%BA%A6" title="时间复杂度">時間複雜度</a>為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {O} (n)\!}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">O</mi>
</mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>n</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mspace width="negativethinmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {O} (n)\!}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathrm {O} (n)\!" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8bc936ac28af050e96d7262b89eb11af36bcc958" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; margin-right: -0.166ex; width:4.792ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>），在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>較大的時候更為顯著。
</p><p>例如計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{100}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>100</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{100}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^{100}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ee422da2d506f653d358806896b1977b638dd00c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.928ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>，普通算法需要算100次，上述算法則只需要算7次。若要計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{n}(n&lt;0)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>&lt;</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{n}(n&lt;0)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^{n} (n &lt; 0)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b44e19e29c71af4d6964ee765c69138bc8750a72" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:9.913ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>可先以上述算法計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a^{|n|}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
</mrow>
<mi>n</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
</mrow>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a^{|n|}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a^{|n|}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/242bf573408f9f54d2aae05b39200bc0380dffc1" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.363ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，再作倒數。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E8.A8.BB.E9.87.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="註釋">註釋</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%86%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：註釋">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Augustin-Louis Cauchy, <i>Cours d'Analyse de l'École Royale Polytechnique</i> (1821).  In his <i>Oeuvres Complètes</i>, series 2, volume 3.</span>
</li>

</li>
<li id="cite_note-Denlinger-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Denlinger_3-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Denlinger, Charles G. Elements of Real Analysis. Jones and Bartlett. 2011: 278–283. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-0-7637-7947-4" title="Special:网络书源/978-0-7637-7947-4"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-0-7637-7947-4</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%86%AA&amp;rft.aufirst=Charles+G.&amp;rft.aulast=Denlinger&amp;rft.btitle=Elements+of+Real+Analysis&amp;rft.date=2011&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-7637-7947-4&amp;rft.pages=278-283&amp;rft.pub=Jones+and+Bartlett&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This definition of a principal root of unity can be found in:
<ul><li><cite class="citation book">Thomas H. Cormen, Charles E. Leiserson, Ronald L. Rivest, and Clifford Stein. Introduction to Algorithms second. MIT Press. 2001. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/0-262-03293-7" title="Special:网络书源/0-262-03293-7"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 0-262-03293-7</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%86%AA&amp;rft.au=Thomas+H.+Cormen%2C+Charles+E.+Leiserson%2C+Ronald+L.+Rivest%2C+and+Clifford+Stein&amp;rft.btitle=Introduction+to+Algorithms&amp;rft.date=2001&amp;rft.edition=second&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=0-262-03293-7&amp;rft.pub=MIT+Press&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span> <a class="external text" href="http://highered.mcgraw-hill.com/sites/0070131511/student_view0/chapter30/glossary.html" rel="nofollow">Online resource</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20070930201902/http://highered.mcgraw-hill.com/sites/0070131511/student_view0/chapter30/glossary.html" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）</li>
<li><cite class="citation book">Paul Cull, Mary Flahive, and Robby Robson. Difference Equations: From Rabbits to Chaos Undergraduate Texts in Mathematics. Springer. 2005. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/0-387-23234-6" title="Special:网络书源/0-387-23234-6"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 0-387-23234-6</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%86%AA&amp;rft.au=Paul+Cull%2C+Mary+Flahive%2C+and+Robby+Robson&amp;rft.btitle=Difference+Equations%3A+From+Rabbits+to+Chaos&amp;rft.date=2005&amp;rft.edition=Undergraduate+Texts+in+Mathematics&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=0-387-23234-6&amp;rft.pub=Springer&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span> Defined on page 351, available on Google books.</li>
<li>"<a class="external text" href="http://mathworld.wolfram.com/PrincipalRootofUnity.html" rel="nofollow">Principal root of unity</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20200805205628/http://mathworld.wolfram.com/PrincipalRootofUnity.html" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）", MathWorld.</li></ul>
</span></li>
</ol></div>
